NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICES
BADRIKUMAR ENTERPRISES PRIVATE LIMITED
R Regd. Off. No. 33 & 34, Mohammed Gani, Rowther Street, Hafizpet, Coimbatore-641 001
Notice is hereby given for general information that the members of the Badrikumar Enterprises Private Limited at
an Extra-ordinary General meeting of the Company held on 28th January 2013 at 10.00 a.m. at the registered office of the
Company at No. 33 & 34, Mohammed Gani, Rowther Street, Hafizpet, Coimbatore-641 001 have passed the following
special resolutions to wind up the above Company voluntarily.
RESOLVED THAT having regard to the declaration made by the Board of Directors dated 31st December 2012
and delivered to the Registrar of Companies under Section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company has
no debts, the company having registered office at No. 33 & 34 Mohammed Gani, Rowther Street, Hafizpet, Coimbatore641 001 be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to Section 484 (1)(b) of the said Act.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT Sri A. Vetrivel B.Sc., F.C.A, Chartered Accountant, having his office at 1/1 Seth
Narayandas Layout II, Tatabad, Coimbatore-641 012 be and is hereby appointed as a Liquidator of the Company pursuant
to the provisions of Section 490, with powers under Section 512 read with Section 457 of the Companies Act, 1956 at a
remuneration of Rs. 10,000/- (Rupees Ten Thousand only) in addition to his costs, charges and expenses.

For Badrikumar Enterprises Private Limited
Coimbatore,
7th February 2013.

K.P. Badrinarayanan,
Managing Director.

BADRIKUMAR ENTERPRISES PRIVATE LIMITED
R Regd. Off. No. 33 & 34, Mohammed Gani, Rowther Street, Hafizpet, Coimbatore-641 001

Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a General Meeting of the Members of above-named
company will be held at Registered Office of the company situated at No. 50, E.V.K. Sampath Salai, Vepery, Chennai-600
007 on Monday the 25th day of February, 2013 at 11.30 A.M. for the purpose of having an account laid before them showing
the manner in which the winding-up has been conducted and the property of the company disposed of and of hearing any
explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by a special resolution of the company, the manner
in which the books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.

Chennai,
7th February 2013.

R. Paranjothi,
Liquidator.
